<A NAME="_Ref369697423"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072126"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left; float:left"><B>10.2</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Negative Covenants</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Until all Loan Obligations owing by the Borrower to 
the Lender have been paid in full, the Borrower agrees with the Lender that it 
will duly perform and comply with each of the following negative covenants 
(except to the extent waived by the Lender):</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072127"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Limitations&nbsp;on&nbsp;Debt.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not create, assume, incur, otherwise
become liable upon, or permit to exist any indebtedness for borrowed money, 
other than:</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
35 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>indebtedness for borrowed money secured by any Permitted Lien 
described in paragraphs&nbsp;(f), (g) and (h) of Subsection 10.2.4;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>indebtedness for borrowed money under any Loan Document; and</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(c)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>unsecured indebtedness for borrowed money owing to a party dealing
at arm&#146;s length with the Borrower at any time not exceeding $100,000 in the
aggregate.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072128"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">10.2.2</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Financial&nbsp;Assistance.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not guarantee the Debt of any other 
person.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072129"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.3</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Sale&nbsp;of&nbsp;Assets.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not dispose of any of its assets, 
except for:</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>disposals of inventory made in the ordinary and usual course of 
carrying on its day to day business; and</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>disposals of used, obsolete, worn-out, damaged, destroyed, or 
surplus equipment in the ordinary course of business and for nominal 
consideration.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref371579354"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072130"></A><A 
NAME="_Ref369691927"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">10.2.4</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Negative&nbsp;Pledge.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not create, incur, assume or 
otherwise become liable upon or permit to exist any Lien on, against or with 
respect to any of its assets, except for:</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>Liens for Taxes and Statutory Prior Claims, assessments or 
governmental charges or levies which are paid when due or, if overdue, the 
validity or amount of which is being contested in good faith by appropriate 
proceedings and in respect of which adequate steps have been taken (which may 
include cash being paid to or pledged with the relevant Governmental Authority) 
to prevent penalties from being imposed, interest from accruing and the 
commencement or continuation of enforcement proceedings and adequate reserves in
accordance with Applicable Accounting Principles have been recorded on the 
consolidated balance sheet of the Borrower;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>mechanics&#146;, carriers&#146;, warehousemen&#146;s, storage, 
repairers&#146; and materialmen&#146;s Liens;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(c)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>Liens or rights of distress reserved in or exercisable under any 
lease for rent not at the time overdue (or, if overdue, such overdue amount is 
being contested in good faith by appropriate proceedings, any exercise of rights
of distress are stayed and adequate reserves required by Applicable Accounting 
Principles are recorded in the accounts and financial statements of the 
Borrower);</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(d)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>customary rights of set-off contained in contracts that are not 
contracts for Debt entered into in the ordinary and usual course of conducting 
day-to-day business;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(e)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>Liens arising solely by virtue of any statutory or common law 
provision relating to banker&#146;s liens, rights of combination of accounts or 
similar rights in the ordinary course of conducting day-to-day banking business 
in relation to deposit </P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; clear:left" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
36 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-left:96px; font-size:12pt"
align=justify>accounts or other funds maintained with a financial institution; 
provided that such Liens (v)&nbsp;do not relate to any deposit account that is a
dedicated cash collateral account which is subject to restrictions against 
access by the depositor or account holder, (w)&nbsp;do not relate to any deposit
account intended by the depositor or account holder to provide collateral to the
depository institution and (x)&nbsp;are not intended directly or indirectly to 
secure the payment or performance of Debt or any other obligation;</P>
<A NAME="_Ref369693129"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; 
width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">(f)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>Liens over specific items of property such as purchasing money 
security interests;</P>
<A NAME="_Ref369693133"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; 
width:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">(g)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>the Liens created by the Security and any other Liens created in 
favour of the Lender; and</P>
<A NAME="_Ref369693138"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; 
width:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">(h)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>such other Liens securing such obligations as may be approved by 
the Lender from time to time.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072131"></A><A NAME="_Ref369691624"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">10.2.5</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>No&nbsp;Merger,&nbsp;Amalgamation,&nbsp;etc.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not enter into any merger, 
amalgamation, arrangement, consolidation, business combination, capital 
reorganization, liquidation, winding-up, dissolution or similar transaction 
(each, a &#147;<B>Business Combination</B>&#148;), unless such Business 
Combination constitutes a Permitted Change of Control.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072132"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.6</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Nature&nbsp;of&nbsp;Business.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not alter the nature of the 
Borrower&#146;s business or cease to carry on any substantial part thereof, nor 
will it engage in any new and unrelated business.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072133"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.7</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Fiscal&nbsp;Year</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower will not change its Fiscal Year end.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072134"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.8</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Constitutional&nbsp;Documents.</I></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;Other than in connection with the Consolidation, the 
Borrower will not amend or modify its Constitutional Documents, except with the 
prior written consent of the Lender.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072135"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">10.2.9</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Exploration&nbsp;and&nbsp;Earn-in&nbsp;Agreement</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower shall not terminate, assign to a third 
party, or change the Exploration and Earn-in Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt" 
align=center><B>ARTICLE&#160;11<BR>
<A NAME="_Toc401072136"></A>EVENTS OF DEFAULT</B></P>
<A NAME="_Ref369691679"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072137"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>11.1</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Events of Default</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>An &#147;<B>Event of Default</B>&#148; shall occur if 
any of the following defaults, breaches, failures, events, states or conditions 
occur or exist at any time.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref371690921"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072138"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">11.1.1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" align=justify><I>Non-
Payment&nbsp;of&nbsp;Principal</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower fails to pay to the Lender any principal 
amount outstanding hereunder when due and such failure continues unremedied for
more than ten (10) Business Days from the date upon which the Lender has 
notified the Borrower in writing of such failure.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072139"></A><A NAME="_Ref369697450"></A><P style="margin-
top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
37 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">11.1.2</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" align=justify><I>Non-
Payment&nbsp;of&nbsp;Interest&nbsp;and&nbsp;Other&nbsp;Amounts</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower fails to pay any interest, fee or other 
amount payable hereunder or under any other Loan Document when due and such 
failure continues unremedied for more than fifteen (15) Business Days from the 
date upon which the Lender has notified the Borrower in writing of such 
failure.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072140"></A><A NAME="_Ref369697456"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">11.1.3</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Misrepresentation</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any representation or warranty made or deemed made by 
the Borrower in any Loan Document is found to have been false or misleading in 
any material respect.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072141"></A><A NAME="_Ref369697468"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">11.1.4</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Breach&nbsp;of&nbsp;Certain&nbsp;Covenants</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower fails to perform or comply with any 
provision or obligation contained in Subsection 10.1.2 or Section 10.2, other 
than Subsection 10.2.4.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072142"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">11.1.5</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Breach&nbsp;of&nbsp;Other&nbsp;Borrower&nbsp;Covenants</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower fails to perform or comply with any 
provision or obligation contained in any Loan Document to which it is a party 
and such failure continues unremedied for a period of forty-five (45) days after
the Lender notifies the Borrower of such failure (other than those referred to 
in Subsections 11.1.1, 11.1.2 and 11.1.4 above).</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072143"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">11.1.6</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Enforcement&nbsp;of&nbsp;Liens</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;Any one or more persons entitled to any Liens on any 
of the Collateral take possession of any material portion of the Collateral or 
any one or more seizures, executions, garnishments, sequestrations, distresses, 
attachments or other equivalent processes are issued or levied against any 
material portion of the Collateral and the Borrower does not discharge the same 
or provide for the discharge in accordance with their terms, or procure a stay 
of execution thereof, within ten (10) days from the date such possession or 
process first takes effect and in any event at least five (5) Business Days
before such Collateral is capable of being disposed of thereunder.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072144"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">11.1.7</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Insolvency</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower takes corporate or other internal 
administrative, management or other governance action to authorize any 
Insolvency Proceeding or any Insolvency Proceeding is commenced against the 
Borrower and such Insolvency Proceeding is not dismissed with thirty (30) days 
of its commencement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072145"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">11.1.8</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Security&nbsp;Imperilled</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;If (17)&nbsp;any Loan Document or any material right 
of the Lender thereunder becomes or is determined by a court of competent 
jurisdiction to be invalid, unenforceable or ineffective, (18)&nbsp;any Security
is determined by a court of competent jurisdiction not to be or ceases to be 
valid and perfected or ranking in priority in the manner contemplated herein or 
in the Security Documents or (19)&nbsp;the Borrower or any receiver of the 
Borrower denies that the Borrower has any or further obligations under any Loan 
Document or challenges the validity of any provision thereof or of the 
Security.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref400437541"></A><A NAME="_Ref400446949"></A><A 
NAME="_Toc401072146"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>11.2</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Termination and Acceleration</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Following the occurrence and during the continuance of
an Event of Default, the Lender may do any one or more of the following:</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>declare the whole or any item or part of the Commitment or any 
unutilized portion of the Loan Facility to be cancelled, terminated or reduced, 
whereupon the Lender </P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; clear:left" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
38 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-left:96px; font-size:12pt"
align=justify>(to the extent applicable) shall not be required to make any 
further Advance available hereunder in respect of such portion of the Commitment
or the Loan Facility cancelled, terminated or reduced;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>accelerate the maturity of all or any item or part of the Loan 
Obligations of the Borrower hereunder and declare them to be payable on demand 
or immediately due and payable, whereupon they shall be so accelerated and 
become so due and payable;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(c)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>suspend any rights of the Borrower under any Loan Document, 
whereupon such rights shall be so suspended;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(d)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>demand payment under any guarantee and/or enforce any Security; or
</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(e)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>take any other action, commence and prosecute any proceeding or 
exercise such other rights as may be permitted by applicable law (whether or not
provided for in any Loan Document) at such times and in such manner as the 
Lender may consider expedient,</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left">all 
without any additional notice, demand, presentment for payment, protest, noting 
of protest, dishonour, notice of dishonour or any other action being required. 
If the Borrower takes corporate or other administrative, management, or other 
governance action to authorize any Insolvency Proceeding, unless the Lender 
otherwise agrees, the Commitment shall be immediately cancelled and the Loan 
Obligations shall be accelerated and become immediately due and payable 
automatically without any action on the part of the Lender being required.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072147"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>11.3</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Waiver</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>The Lender may waive any Default. No waiver, however, 
shall be deemed to extend to a subsequent Default, whether or not the same as or
similar to the Default waived, and no act or omission by the Lender shall extend
to, or be taken in any manner whatsoever to affect, any subsequent Default or 
the rights of the Lender arising therefrom. Any such waiver must be in writing 
and signed by the Lender to be effective. No failure on the part of the Lender 
to exercise, and no delay by the Lender in exercising, any rights under any Loan
Document shall operate as a waiver of such rights. No single or partial exercise
of any such rights shall preclude any other or further exercise of such rights 
or the exercise of any other rights.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072148"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>11.4</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Performance of the Borrower&#146;s Obligations by the 
Lender</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>If the Borrower fails to perform any obligation to be 
performed by it in the timeline provided therefor pursuant to any Loan Document 
and such failure continues for ten (10) Business Days after the Lender notifies 
the Borrower of such failure, the Lender may in its sole discretion, after 
written notice to the Borrower, perform such obligation but shall be under no 
obligation to do so, and any amount expended or advanced by the Lender for such 
purpose shall be reimbursed by the Borrower to the Lender upon demand together 
with interest at the Default Rate accruing from the date such amount was so 
expended or advanced.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072149"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" 
align=justify><BR>

39 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left"><B>11.5</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Press Releases </B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Subject to compliance with applicable laws, any press 
release of the Borrower relating to the Loan will be provided in advance to the 
Lender, and the Borrower will use its commercially reasonable efforts to agree 
to the form and content thereof with the Lender, prior to the release 
thereof.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072150"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>11.6</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Cancellation of Warrants</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>On the First Closing, the 6,500,000 warrants issued to
Look Back Investments Inc., expiring on December 31, 2013, were cancelled.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt" 
align=center><B>ARTICLE&#160;12<BR>
<A NAME="_Toc401072151"></A>GENERAL</B></P>
<A NAME="_Ref400444896"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072152"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.1</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Costs and Expenses</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Whether or not the transactions contemplated by this 
Agreement are completed or any Advance is made hereunder, the Borrower shall on 
demand pay to the Lender the amount of all reasonable out-of-pocket fees, costs 
and expenses incurred or payable and disbursements made by the Lender (including
the reasonable fees and out-of-pocket expenses of the Lender&#146;s counsel and 
those of accountants, experts, consultants and other representatives retained by
the Lender) (20)&nbsp;up to the maximum amount of $40,000 for its Canadian 
counsel (not including disbursements and applicable taxes) and up to a maximum 
of $10,000 for Erwin &amp; Thompson LLP (not including disbursements and 
applicable taxes) in connection with each of&nbsp;due diligence expense, the 
preparation, negotiation, settlement, execution, delivery, entry into effect of 
each Loan Document and/or the satisfaction of any conditions or obligations 
specified in Section 7.2, and (21)&nbsp;in connection with (y)&nbsp;post-closing
costs, (z)&nbsp;each change to each Loan Document and (aa)&nbsp;the 
interpretation, defence, establishment, preservation, protection or enforcement 
of rights of the Lender under each Loan Document. The Borrower hereby authorizes
the Lender to deduct all such fees, costs and expenses from any Advance to be 
made on or subsequent to the Second Closing Date, and shall supply proper 
invoices supporting the same.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref400444915"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072153"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.2</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Indemnification by the Borrower</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072154"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">12.2.1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Advances</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower shall indemnify and save harmless the 
Lender on a full indemnity basis from and against all claims and losses and
expenses which the Lender sustains or incurs (22)&nbsp;if for any reason an 
Advance does not occur on a date requested by the Borrower, unless the Advance 
does not occur by reason of the breach by the Lender of its obligations under 
this Agreement, (23)&nbsp;if the Borrower fails to give any notice required to 
be given by it hereunder in the manner and at the time specified herein, or 
(24)&nbsp;as a consequence of any failure by the Borrower to repay any amount 
when required by the terms of this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072155"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.2.2</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Other</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower shall defend, indemnify and save harmless
the Lender and its representatives (each, an &#147;<B>Indemnified 
Party</B>&#148;) on a full indemnity basis from and against any and all claims 
and losses and expenses (including interest and, to the extent permitted by 
applicable law, penalties, fines and monetary sanctions) which an Indemnified 
Party suffers or incurs as a result of or otherwise in respect of (25)&nbsp;any 
claim of any kind relating to the </P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
40 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>Environment which arises out of the performance of, or the 
enforcement or exercise of any right under, any Loan Document, including any 
claim in nuisance, negligence, strict liability or other cause of action arising
out of a discharge of contaminants into the Environment, any fines or orders of 
any kind that may be levied or made pursuant to an Environmental Law in each 
case relating to or otherwise arising out of any Collateral, (26)&nbsp;the 
direct or indirect use or proposed use of the proceeds of any Advance, 
(27)&nbsp;any Default or (28)&nbsp;any proceeding to which any Indemnified Party
is party arising out of the execution, delivery or performance of, or the 
enforcement of any right under any Loan Document. &nbsp;The Lender shall be 
constituted as the agent and bare trustee of each Indemnified Party who is its 
own representative and shall hold and enforce each such Indemnified Party&#146;s
rights under this paragraph for such party&#146;s benefit. The foregoing 
indemnity shall not apply in respect of claims or losses and expenses of an 
Indemnified Party to the extent that they are determined by a final judgment to 
have directly resulted from the gross negligence or wilful misconduct of that 
Indemnified Party.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072156"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.3</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Application of Payments</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Any payments received by the Lender in respect of the 
Loan Obligations from time to time may, notwithstanding any appropriation by the
Borrower, be appropriated to such parts of the Loan Obligations then due and 
owing by the Borrower to the Lender and in such order as the Lender sees fit, 
and the Lender shall have the right to change any appropriation at any time.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072157"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.4</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Set-Off</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>The Loan Obligations will be paid by the Borrower
without regard to any equities between the Borrower and the Lender or any right 
of set-off or counterclaim. Any Debt owing by the Lender to the Borrower, direct
or indirect, extended or renewed, actual or contingent, matured or not, may be 
set-off or applied against, or combined with, the Loan Obligations by the Lender
at any time, either before or after maturity, without demand upon or notice to 
anyone, and the terms of such Debt shall be changed hereby to the extent 
required to permit such set-off, application and combination. The Lender agrees 
not to effect any such set-off, application or combination of accounts against 
Loan Obligations not yet due unless (29)&nbsp;an Event of Default has occurred 
and is continuing or (30)&nbsp;the Lender is or is reasonably likely to be 
materially prejudiced by not doing so.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072158"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.5</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Rights in Addition</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>The rights conferred by each Loan Document are in 
addition to, and not in substitution for, any other rights the Lender may have 
under that Loan Document or any other Loan Document, at law, in equity or by or 
under applicable law or any agreement. The Lender may proceed by way of any 
proceeding at law or in equity and no right of the Lender shall be exclusive of 
or dependent on any other. The Lender may exercise any of its rights separately 
or in combination and at any time.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072159"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" 
align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>

41 -</P>

<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left"><B>12.6</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Certificate Evidence</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>A certificate prepared by the Lender and provided to 
the Borrower setting forth any interest rate or any amount payable under any 
Loan Document shall constitute <I>prima facie</I> evidence thereof, absent 
manifest error.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072160"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.7</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Evidence of Debt</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>The Lender shall open and maintain on its books 
accounts evidencing all Advances under the Loan Facility and all amounts owing 
by the Borrower to the Lender under the Loan Facility. The Lender shall enter in
the accounts details of all amounts from time to time owing, paid or repaid by 
the Borrower under the Loan Facility. The information entered in the accounts 
shall constitute, in the absence of manifest error, <I>prima facie</I> evidence 
of the existence and quantum of the obligations of the Borrower to the Lender 
under the Loan Facility. The Borrower shall, on reasonable notice to the Lender,
be entitled to obtain promptly from the Lender copies of extracts of all entries
made in such accounts.</P>

<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt"

<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt;

communication to be made or given under or in connection with this Agreement (a

provided that the party sending such Notice receives confirmation of receipt
from the recipient&#146;s telecopy machine or e-mail server. Notwithstanding the
foregoing, (31)&nbsp;the Lender may in its discretion act upon verbal Notice 
from any person reasonably believed by the Lender to be a person authorized by 
the Borrower to give instructions under or in connection with this Agreement, 
including any request by the Borrower for an Advance and (32)&nbsp;any Notice 
received by the Lender on a day which is not a Business Day or after noon on any

<A NAME="_Ref400444945"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072162"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.9</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Judgment Currency</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>If, for the purposes of obtaining or enforcing 
judgment in any court in any jurisdiction, it becomes necessary to convert into 
the currency of the jurisdiction giving such judgment (the &#147;<B>Judgment 
Currency</B>&#148;) an amount due under any Loan Document in any other currency 
(the &#147;<B>Original Currency</B>&#148;), then the date on which the rate of 
exchange for conversion is selected by that court is referred to herein as the 
&#147;<B>Conversion Date</B>&#148;. If there is a change in the rate of exchange
between the Judgment Currency and the Original Currency between the Conversion 
Date and the actual receipt by the Lender of the amount due to it under such 
Loan Document or under such judgment, the Borrower shall, notwithstanding such 
judgment, pay all such additional amounts as may be necessary to ensure that the
amount received by the Lender in the Judgment Currency, when converted at the 
rate of exchange prevailing on the date of receipt, </P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" align=justify><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt; page-break-before:always" align=center>- 
43 -</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt" align=justify>will
produce the amount due in the Original Currency. &nbsp;The Borrower&#146;s 
liability hereunder constitutes a separate and independent liability which shall
not merge with any judgment or any partial payment or enforcement of payment of 
sums due under this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref369699142"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072163"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.10</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Successors and Assigns</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072164"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">12.10.1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Benefit&nbsp;&amp;&nbsp;Burden</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Loan Documents shall enure to the benefit of and 
be binding on the parties thereto, their respective successors, and each 
assignee of some or all of the rights or obligations of the parties under the 
Loan Documents permitted by this Section 12.10. Any reference in any such Loan 
Document to any party thereto shall (to the extent the context so admits) be 
construed accordingly.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072165"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.10.2</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Borrower</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower may not assign all or any part of any of
its rights or obligations in respect of the Loan Facility or under any Loan 
Document.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072166"></A><A NAME="_Ref369691887"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">12.10.3</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Participation</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Lender may grant a participation (whether by way 
of equitable assignment, limited recourse deposit or otherwise) to any other 
person (a &#147;<B>Participant</B>&#148;) in the whole or any part of any of its
Commitments under which the Participant shall be entitled to the benefit of the 
same rights under this Agreement with respect to such Participation as if it 
were a party hereto in the place and stead of the Lender.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072167"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.10.4</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Assignments</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Lender may assign any of its Commitments 
(including its rights and obligations and any related Advances made thereunder),
or any part thereof, or any Advances, or part thereof, to any other person.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072168"></A><A NAME="_Ref369699172"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">12.10.5</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Disclosure</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Lender may disclose to any prospective or actual 
Participant in or assignee of any rights or obligations in respect of the Loan 
Facility any information regarding the Borrower, its assets or any of its 
business affairs so long as the prospective or actual Participant or assignee 
agrees to be bound by the confidentiality provisions of this Subsection 12.10.5.
The Lender shall keep confidential and not disclose to any third party 
(excluding for certainty its own representatives, professional advisors and 
affiliates) any confidential information received by the Lender from the 
Borrower pursuant to this Agreement, save that the Lender may disclose any such 
confidential information (33)&nbsp;as provided in the preceding sentence, 
(34)&nbsp;to the extent required by applicable law, (35)&nbsp;to the extent 
required to protect the rights of the Lender in any actual, pending or 
threatened proceeding, or (36)&nbsp;as may be necessary or desirable in order to
enforce the rights of the Lender under any Loan Document.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072169"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.11</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Survival</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>The obligations of the Borrower under Sections 4.3, 
12.1, 12.2 and 12.9 shall survive the payment and performance in full of all 
other Loan Obligations owing by the Borrower to the Lender and shall continue in
full force and effect until such obligations are irrevocably paid and performed 
in full.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072170"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.12</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Time of the Essence</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>Time is of the essence of each provision of each Loan 
Document.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072171"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px" 
align=justify><BR>

<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-

float:left"><B>12.13</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Governing Law</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>This Agreement shall be governed by, and construed and
interpreted in accordance with, the laws in force in the State of Nevada. Such 
choice of law shall, however, be without prejudice to or limitation of any other
rights available to the Lender under the laws of any jurisdiction where the 
Borrower or its assets may be located.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref369699270"></A><A NAME="_Toc401072172"></A><P style=margin-
top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-
bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.14</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Jurisdiction</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072173"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">12.14.1</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Submission&nbsp;to&nbsp;Jurisdiction&nbsp;and&nbsp;Waiver&nbsp;
of&nbsp;Objections</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;Save as otherwise herein provided, with respect to any
claim arising out of this Agreement, any other Loan Document or any other 
agreement relating to any Loan Document (in this Section 12.14, collectively, 
the &#147;<B>Secured Related Documents</B>&#148;) for the exclusive benefit of 
the Lender, the Borrower irrevocably and unconditionally submits, for itself and
its property, to the non-exclusive jurisdiction of the Sixth Judicial District 
Court of State of Nevada, Pershing County, Nevada, including any appellate court
therefrom (in this Section 12.14, &#147;<B>Courts of Primary 
Jurisdiction</B>&#148;). &nbsp;The Borrower irrevocably waives (bb)&nbsp;any 
objection which it may have at any time to the laying of venue of any proceeding
arising out of or relating to any of the Secured Related Documents brought in 
any Court of Primary Jurisdiction, (cc)&nbsp;any claim that any such proceeding 
brought in any Court of Primary Jurisdiction has been brought in an inconvenient
forum, (dd)&nbsp;the right to object, with respect to such proceeding brought in
any Court of Primary Jurisdiction, that such court does not have jurisdiction 
over the Borrower and (ee)&nbsp;the right to require the Lender to post security
for costs in any proceeding brought in any Court of Primary Jurisdiction.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072174"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.14.2</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Lender&nbsp;May&nbsp;Sue&nbsp;in&nbsp;Another&nbsp;Jurisdiction
</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;Nothing in this Agreement will be deemed to preclude 
the Lender from bringing any proceeding in respect of any Secured Related 
Document in any other jurisdiction.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072175"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.14.3</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Final&nbsp;Judgment</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower agrees that a final judgment in any
proceeding commenced in any Court of Primary Jurisdiction shall be conclusive 
and may be enforced in any other jurisdictions by suit on the judgment or in any
other manner provided by law.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072176"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left">12.14.4</P>
<P style="margin:0px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><I>Manner&nbsp;of&nbsp;Service</I>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" 
align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;The Borrower irrevocably consents to the service of 
process out of the Courts of Primary Jurisdiction in accordance with the local 
rules of civil procedure or by mailing a copy thereof, by registered mail, 
postage prepaid to the Borrower at the address of the Borrower, or by sending a 
copy thereof by facsimile or e-mail in PDF format to the Borrower at the 
facsimile number or e-mail address of the Borrower determined under Section 
12.8.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072177"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:96px; font-
size:12pt; float:left"><B>12.15</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Invalidity</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>If any provision of any Loan Document is determined to
be invalid or unenforceable by a final judgment, that provision shall be deemed 
to be severed therefrom, and the remaining provisions of such Loan Document 
shall not be affected thereby and shall remain valid and enforceable. The 
parties hereto shall, at the request of the Lender, negotiate in good faith with
the Lender to replace any invalid or unenforceable provision contained in any 
Loan Document with a valid and enforceable provision which has the commercial 
effect as close as possible to that of the invalid or unenforceable provision, 
to the extent permitted by law.</P>

<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>Changes</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>No agreement purporting to change (other than waive) 
any provision of any Loan Document shall be binding upon the parties hereto or 
thereto unless that agreement is in writing and signed by the Lender and the 
Borrower. No waiver of strict performance or compliance with any provision of 
any Loan Document shall be binding on any party hereto or thereto unless such 
waiver is in writing signed by the party sought to be bound thereby.</P>

<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt"

<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>There are no representations, warranties, conditions, 
other agreements or acknowledgments, whether direct or collateral, express or 
implied, binding on the Lender that form part of or affect this Agreement or any
other Loan Document, other than as expressed herein or in such other Loan 
Document. The execution of each Loan Document by the Borrower has not been 
induced by, nor does the Borrower rely upon or regard as material, any
representations, warranties, conditions, other agreements or acknowledgments not
expressly made in any Loan Document.</P>

<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>If there is any inconsistency between the provisions 
of this Agreement and the provisions of any other Loan Document to which the 
Borrower is party, the provisions hereof shall govern and apply to the extent of
the inconsistency.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc401072181"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-

clear:left" align=justify>This Agreement may be executed in any number of 
counterparts, each of which shall be deemed to be an original and all of which 
taken together shall be deemed to constitute one and the same instrument, and it
shall not be necessary in making proof of this Agreement to produce or account 
for more than one such counterpart. Transmission of a copy of an executed 
signature page of this Agreement (including any change to this Agreement) by one
party hereto to the other party hereto by facsimile transmission or e-mail in

<P style="margin:0px; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>PROMISSORY NOTE</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px"><BR></P>
</DIV><TABLE style="margin-top:0px; font-size:10pt" cellpadding=0

<DIV style="width:624px"><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify><B>FOR VALUE RECEIVED,</B> <B>LIBERTY SILVER CORP. </B>(herein 
called the &#147;<B>Issuer</B>&#148;), a corporation formed under the laws of 
the State of Nevada, hereby acknowledges itself indebted to and promises to pay 
on the earlier of the Second Maturity Date and the Acceleration Date to or to 
the order of<B> BG CAPITAL GROUP LTD.</B> (herein called the 
&#147;<B>Holder</B>&#148;), a company formed under the laws of Barbados, the 
lesser (the &#147;<B>Outstanding Principal Amount</B>&#148;) of (i)&nbsp;the 
principal sum of <B>ONE MILLION TWO HUNDRED AND FIFTY THOUSAND U.S. DOLLARS 
</B>($1,250,000)<B> </B>or (ii)&nbsp;the Loan Amount owing from time to time by 
the Issuer under the Loan Agreement, and to pay interest from September 30, 2014
on the Outstanding Principal Amount until the Outstanding Principal Amount and 
all accrued and unpaid interest thereon payable hereunder is paid in full to the
Holder calculated and payable as follows:</P>
<A NAME="_Ref284514508"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; 
width:96px; font-size:12pt; float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>subject to paragraph (b), interest shall accrue on the Outstanding
Principal Amount at the rate of (x) eleven percent (11%) per annum from 
September 30, 2014 until October&nbsp;14, 2015 (inclusively), and (y) fifteen 
percent (15%) per annum from October 15, 2015 and anytime thereafter (as 
applicable, the &#147;<B>Interest Rate</B>&#148;);</P>
<A NAME="_Ref284514250"></A><P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-
size:1pt /><P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; 
width:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left; float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>interest shall accrue at the rate equal to the applicable Interest
Rate plus five percent (5%) (the &#147;<B>Default Rate</B>&#148;) on any amount 
(including without limitation principal or interest) payable under this Note 
which is not paid on the date it is or becomes due and payable hereunder until 
such unpaid amount is paid in full to the Holder; </P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt;
clear:left; float:left">(c)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>interest payable hereunder shall accrue from day to day, be 
payable in arrears in lawful currency of the United States of America and be 
computed upon the daily balance of the Outstanding Principal Amount and shall be
calculated on the basis of the actual number of days elapsed in a year of 365 or
366 days, as the case may be; and</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(d)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>interest accrued at the Interest Rate or Default Rate, as the case
may be, shall be due and payable on each Interest Payment Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left" align=justify>This Note evidences the amounts owing by the Issuer to
the Holder under the Loan Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px"><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:8pt">Promissory Note - LIBERTY SILVER CORP.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; page-break-before:always"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-
size:12pt"><B><I>Payments</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>All payments under this Note shall be made &nbsp;free and clear 
of, and without regard for, any existing or future rights of counterclaim, 
defence, set-off, compensation, abatement, offset or cross-claim, legal or 
equitable, of any nature or kind that may exist between the parties to this Note
in lawful currency of the United States of America to the credit of such account
of the Holder maintained with such branch of such financial institution as the 
Holder shall from time to time notify the Issuer.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt"><B><I>No 
Prepayment</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>The Issuer shall have the right to prepay the Outstanding 
Principal Amount, in whole or in part, with the payment of a prepayment fee to 
the Holder equal to five percent (5%) of the Outstanding Principal Amount being 
prepaid. &nbsp;Any partial prepayment must be in the minimum principal amount of
$50,000.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt"><B><I>Withholding 
Taxes</I></B></P>
<A NAME="_Ref11242314"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:96px; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Each payment required to be made by 
the Issuer under this Note shall be made free and clear of, and without 
deduction or withholding for or on account of, any Indemnified Taxes, except to 
the extent such deduction or withholding is required by any applicable law, as 
modified by the administrative practice of any relevant Governmental Authority, 
then in effect. &nbsp;To the extent and each time the Issuer is so required to 
deduct or withhold Indemnified Taxes from or in respect of any such payment to 
or for the account of the Holder, then the Issuer will:</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(a)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>promptly notify the Holder of such requirement;</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(b)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>pay to the relevant Governmental Authority when due the full 
amount required to be deducted or withheld (including the full amount of
Indemnified Taxes required to be deducted or withheld from any additional amount
paid by the Issuer to or for the account of the Holder under this 
provision);</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(c)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>promptly forward to the Holder an official receipt (or a certified
copy), or other documentation reasonably acceptable to the Holder, evidencing 
such payment to such Governmental Authority; and</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:48px; width:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(d)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:96px; text-indent:-2px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>forthwith pay to the Holder, in addition to the payment to which 
the Holder is otherwise entitled under this Note, such additional amount as is 
necessary to ensure that the net amount actually received by the Holder (free 
and clear of, and net of, any such Indemnified Taxes, including the full amount 
of Taxes required to be deducted or withheld from any additional amount paid by 
the Issuer under this provision, whether assessed against the Issuer or the 
Holder) will equal the full amount the Holder would have received had no such 
deduction or withholding been required.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref72657377"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:96px; font-size:12pt; clear:left" align=justify>If the Issuer fails to 
pay to the relevant Governmental Authority when due any Indemnified Taxes that 
it was required to deduct or withhold under the preceding paragraph in respect 
of any payment to or for the benefit of the Holder under this Note, or fails to 
promptly </P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px"><BR>
<BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-size:8pt">Promissory Note - LIBERTY SILVER CORP.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<HR style="margin-bottom:9.6px; padding-top:9.6px" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="margin:0px; page-break-before:always"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>furnish the Holder with the documentation referred to in the 
preceding paragraph, the Issuer shall forthwith on demand indemnify the Holder 
on a full indemnity after-Taxes basis from and against the full amount of any 
Taxes (including interest and penalties), losses and expenses which the Holder 
may suffer or incur as a result of such failure.</P>
<A NAME="_Ref72657402"></A><P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:96px; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Issuer shall also indemnify the 
Holder on a full indemnity after-Tax basis, for any additional Taxes on net 
income that the Holder may be obliged to pay as a result of the payment of 
additional amounts under the preceding paragraphs.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-
size:12pt"><B><I>Acceleration</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>If an Event of Default occurs, then unless the Holder notifies the
Issuer to the contrary, the Outstanding Principal Amount, accrued interest and 
all other amounts payable by the Issuer provided for herein shall become 
immediately due and payable.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:12pt"><B><I>Records of 
Account</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt" 
align=justify>A record of the principal and accrued interest payable hereunder 
and payments of principal and interest may, at the Holder&#146;s sole option, be
entered:</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:96px; width:144px; font-size:12pt; 
float:left">(i)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:144px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:12pt"align=justify>in any electronic data processing device, and any 
printed report produced from such electronic records shall be good and 
sufficient evidence of the unpaid principal and interest balance in the same 
manner and to the same extent as if originally and concurrently recorded on or 
with this Note. &nbsp;The Holder is under no obligation to retain original 
vouchers related to any such entry; or</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:96px; width:144px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(ii)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:144px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:12pt"align=justify>by the Holder on the grid annexed hereto; or</P>
<P style=margin-top:16px;margin-bottom:-1pt;font-size:1pt /><P style="margin-
top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; text-indent:96px; width:144px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left; float:left">(iii)</P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:144px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:12pt"align=justify>in any combination of the methods outlined in 
subparagraphs&nbsp;(i) and (ii) above.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-size:12pt; 
clear:left"align=justify>Failure to record the date and amount of any principal 
amount which the Issuer has agreed to pay under this Note, or any accrued 
interest or payments made hereunder, shall not limit or otherwise affect the 
obligations of the Issuer to pay this Note.</P>
<P style="margin-top:16px; margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:96px; font-
size:12pt"align=justify>The Holder is hereby irrevocably authorized by the 
Issuer as the Issuer&#146;s lawful attorney and agent (with full power of 
substitution and delegation) to endorse on the grid attached to this Note such 
amount of principal advanced by the Holder to the Issuer under the Loan 
Agreement from time to time, interest accrued thereon and all other amounts 
payable under the Loan Agreement and the amount of each payment of principal, 
interest and other amounts received by the Holder under the Loan Agreement as 
well as the dates thereof. &nbsp;The failure of the Holder to make any such 
endorsement shall not release or otherwise alter the Issuer&#146;s obligations 
hereunder to repay the principal of this Note, other amounts and accrued 
interest thereon payable hereunder. &nbsp;The unpaid principal, other amounts 
and accrued interest payable under this Note recorded in the grid and/or the 
printed report from any electronic data processing device of the Holder shall be
conclusive and binding on the Issuer absent manifest error and may be introduced
as evidence of the amount owing by the Issuer hereunder. &nbsp;</P>
